***onpartijdig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onpartijdig.html>onpartijdig</a> (23732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-, non-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:partijdig.html>partijdig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">partial, partisan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onpartijdig.html>onpartijdig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onpartijdig.html>onpartijdiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">onpartijdigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>not being affiliated to a stakeholder, impartial, unpartisan</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of persons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> impartial, unbiased, treating all parties, rivals or disputants equally
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">onbevooroordeeld</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> not tainted by partiality or prejudice

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onrustig.html>onrustig</a> (10400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rustig.html>rustig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quiet, calm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onrustig.html>onrustig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onrustiger.html>onrustiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">onrustigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>restless, agitated, unsettled</li>

***ons.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> (73)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unsiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>us (objective form of <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagelijks.html>dagelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Give <b>us</b> today our daily bread.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*unsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unseraz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>, <i>inflected form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>our <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuter</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagelijks.html>dagelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give us <b>our</b> daily bread</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Only used with singular neuter nouns in dependent clauses; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in all other situations as an independent possessive as well as with male and female nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">unce</i> (1240), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">uncia</i> (a twelfth of a pound) probably <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">once</i>. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">onsen</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onzen.html>onzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onsje.html>onsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">metric ounce</span> (100 <span class="Latn" lang="en">grams</span>)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Prior to the law of 1820 that introduced the metric system in what then united both the Netherlands and Belgium a variety of measures ranging around ca 30 grams <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> known by this name. The law of 1820 attributed the name to the hectogram of 100 grams. In 1937 the IJkwet of the Netherlands officially abolished the term, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still commonly used.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hectogram</span></li></ul>

</li>
</ol></div>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ontbēren</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*beraną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinden.html>ontbinden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">antbindan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*andabindaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binden.html>binden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinden.html>ontbinden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unbind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dissolve, break up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decompose</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a> (18006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinden.html>ontbinden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to decompose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbindingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Decomposition (e.g. of organic matter or in mathematics).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kadaver.html>kadaver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkeert.html>verkeert</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a>.</b>
<dl><dd><i>The cadaver <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> decomposing.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 46 in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> priemfactoren <a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> 23.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The decomposition of 46 into its underlying primes yields 2 and 23.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>Dissolution (e.g. of a legal entity).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vereniging.html>vereniging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vond.html>vond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> in 1931.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The dissolution of the society <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> place in 1931.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">telbaar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">countable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontelbaar.html>ontelbaar</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>uncountable, which cannot be counted, expressed numerically
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">telbaar</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>innumerable, of very great number</li></ol>

***ontfermen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontfermen.html>ontfermen</a> (22475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">entfarmen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ontfarmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*intfarmon</i>, with two prefixes <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> attached to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*armāną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a></i> derives from the same source, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Old High German and with a different prefix. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">arm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontfermen.html>ontfermen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take pity [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = on]</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***ontheemd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontheemd.html>ontheemd</a> (53656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-, de-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">heem</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">home</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Coined in 1944 as a translation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">displaced person</i>. While it resembles a participle morphologically, it does not derive from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onthemen</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> in fact seen some (<a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>) usage but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> itself a <span class="Latn" lang="en">back-formation</span> from this adjective.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontheemd.html>ontheemd</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of people</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">displaced</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">deprived</span> of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">home</span></li></ol>

***onthoofden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onthoofden.html>onthoofden</a> (13920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onthôveden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">de-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onthoofden.html>onthoofden</a></strong>
</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>To behead, decapitate, notably as capital punishment
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">onthalzen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To remove the leadership, the brains etc. (from ...)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>Zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorzitter.html>voorzitter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onthoofde.html>onthoofde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:raad.html>raad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluiteloos.html>besluiteloos</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>Without its chairman, the headless board <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indecisive</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onthoofding.html>onthoofding</a></span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a> (2292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep in mind, to remember
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgende.html>volgende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a>.</i> — I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> <b>keep</b> it <b>in mind</b> for the next time.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">arithmetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>, 3 <a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> 5, <a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a> 8 <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a> 1!</i> — Let's see, carry 3, divide by 5, times 8 <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> 1!</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to retain, to withhold
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onthield.html>onthield</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>, want <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mening.html>mening</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>.</i> — I <b>retained</b> my vote, because I <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>haven</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> got an opinion about this case.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deny
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plezier.html>plezier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a></i> — You can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> deny him that pleasure.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to abstain
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:vasten.html>Vasten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheel.html>geheel</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:gedeeltelijk.html>gedeeltelijk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onthouden.html>onthouden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:periode.html>periode</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasten">[1]</a></sup>  |  Fasting <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the entire or partial abstention from eating or drinking for a certain period.</dd></dl></li></ol>
